          <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
           <p>
            Is there a "canonical" way of doing that? I've been using
            <code>
             head -n | tail -1
            </code>
            which does the trick, but I've been wondering if there's a Bash tool that specifically extracts a line (or a range of lines) from a file.
           </p>
           <p>
            By "canonical" I mean a program whose main function is doing that.
           </p>

        <div class="answer js-answer accepted-answer" data-answerid="6022431" data-highest-scored="1" data-parentid="6022384" data-position-on-page="1" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="1012" id="answer-6022431" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="6022431">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="1012" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             1012
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/6022431/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <code>
              head
             </code>
             and pipe with
             <code>
              tail
             </code>
             will be slow for a huge file. I would suggest
             <code>
              sed
             </code>
             like this:
            </p>
            <pre><code>sed 'NUMq;d' file
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Where
             <code>
              NUM
             </code>
             is the number of the line you want to print; so, for example,
             <code>
              sed '10q;d' file
             </code>
             to print the 10th line of
             <code>
              file
             </code>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             Explanation:
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              NUMq
             </code>
             will quit immediately when the line number is
             <code>
              NUM
             </code>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              d
             </code>
             will delete the line instead of printing it; this is inhibited on the last line because the
             <code>
              q
             </code>
             causes the rest of the script to be skipped when quitting.
            </p>
            <p>
             If you have
             <code>
              NUM
             </code>
             in a variable, you will want to use double quotes instead of single:
            </p>
            <pre><code>sed "${NUM}q;d" file
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

                 <code>
                  sed -n 'NUMp'
                 </code>
                 and
                 <code>
                  sed 'NUM!d'
                 </code>
                 solutions proposed below.

                 <code>
                  tail -n+NUM file | head -n1
                 </code>
                 is likely to be just as fast or faster. At least, it was (significantly) faster on my system when I tried it with NUM being 250000 on a file with half a million lines. YMMV, but I don't really see why it would.

          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="6022441">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/6022441/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <pre><code>sed -n '2p' &lt; file.txt
</code></pre>
            <p>
             will print 2nd line
            </p>
            <pre><code>sed -n '2011p' &lt; file.txt
</code></pre>
            <p>
             2011th line
            </p>
            <pre><code>sed -n '10,33p' &lt; file.txt
</code></pre>
            <p>
             line 10 up to line 33
            </p>
            <pre><code>sed -n '1p;3p' &lt; file.txt
</code></pre>
            <p>
             1st and 3th line
            </p>
            <p>
             and so on...
            </p>
            <p>
             For adding lines with sed, you can check this:
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/q/15555781/#16246806">
              sed: insert a line in a certain position
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 @RafaelBarbosa the
                 <code>
                  &lt;
                 </code>
                 in this case is not necessary. Simply, it is my preference using redirects, because me often used redirects like
                 <code>
                  sed -n '100p' &lt; &lt;(some_command)
                 </code>
                 - so, universal syntax :). It is NOT less effective, because redirection are done with shell when forking itself, so... it is only a preference... (and yes, it is one character longer) :)
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/632407/jm666" title="58,473 reputation">

              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 This is about 5 times slower than the tail / head combination when reading a file with 50M rows
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/1727392/duhaime" title="22,754 reputation">
                  duhaime
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2018-06-04 14:42:24Z, License: CC BY-SA 4.0">

             </li>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="39217130" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="6022384" data-position-on-page="3" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="117" id="answer-39217130" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="39217130">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="117" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             117
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/39217130/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I have a unique situation where I can benchmark the solutions proposed on this page, and so I'm writing this answer as a consolidation of the proposed solutions with included run times for each.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Set Up
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             I have a 3.261 gigabyte ASCII text data file with one key-value pair per row. The file contains 3,339,550,320 rows in total and defies opening in any editor I have tried, including my go-to Vim. I need to subset this file in order to investigate some of the values that I've discovered only start around row ~500,000,000.
            </p>
            <p>
             Because the file has so many rows:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              I need to extract only a subset of the rows to do anything useful with the data.
             </li>
             <li>
              Reading through every row leading up to the values I care about is going to take a long time.
             </li>
             <li>
              If the solution reads past the rows I care about and continues reading the rest of the file it will waste time reading almost 3 billion irrelevant rows and take 6x longer than necessary.
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             My best-case-scenario is a solution that extracts only a single line from the file without reading any of the other rows in the file, but I can't think of how I would accomplish this in Bash.
            </p>
            <p>
             For the purposes of my sanity I'm not going to be trying to read the full 500,000,000 lines I'd need for my own problem. Instead I'll be trying to extract row 50,000,000 out of 3,339,550,320 (which means reading the full file will take 60x longer than necessary).
            </p>
            <p>
             I will be using the
             <code>
              time
             </code>
             built-in to benchmark each command.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Baseline
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             First let's see how the
             <code>
              head
             </code>
             <code>
              tail
             </code>
             solution:
            </p>
            <pre><code>$ time head -50000000 myfile.ascii | tail -1
pgm_icnt = 0

real    1m15.321s
</code></pre>
            <p>
             The baseline for row 50 million is 00:01:15.321, if I'd gone straight for row 500 million it'd probably be ~12.5 minutes.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              cut
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             I'm dubious of this one, but it's worth a shot:
            </p>
            <pre><code>$ time cut -f50000000 -d$'\n' myfile.ascii
pgm_icnt = 0

real    5m12.156s
</code></pre>
            <p>
             This one took 00:05:12.156 to run, which is much slower than the baseline! I'm not sure whether it read through the entire file or just up to line 50 million before stopping, but regardless this doesn't seem like a viable solution to the problem.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              AWK
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             I only ran the solution with the
             <code>
              exit
             </code>
             because I wasn't going to wait for the full file to run:
            </p>
            <pre><code>$ time awk 'NR == 50000000 {print; exit}' myfile.ascii
pgm_icnt = 0

real    1m16.583s
</code></pre>
            <p>
             This code ran in 00:01:16.583, which is only ~1 second slower, but still not an improvement on the baseline. At this rate if the exit command had been excluded it would have probably taken around ~76 minutes to read the entire file!
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Perl
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             I ran the existing Perl solution as well:
            </p>
            <pre><code>$ time perl -wnl -e '$.== 50000000 &amp;&amp; print &amp;&amp; exit;' myfile.ascii
pgm_icnt = 0

real    1m13.146s
</code></pre>
            <p>
             This code ran in 00:01:13.146, which is ~2 seconds faster than the baseline. If I'd run it on the full 500,000,000 it would probably take ~12 minutes.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              sed
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             The top answer on the board, here's my result:
            </p>
            <pre><code>$ time sed "50000000q;d" myfile.ascii
pgm_icnt = 0

real    1m12.705s
</code></pre>
            <p>
             This code ran in 00:01:12.705, which is 3 seconds faster than the baseline, and ~0.4 seconds faster than Perl. If I'd run it on the full 500,000,000 rows it would have probably taken ~12 minutes.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              mapfile
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             I have bash 3.1 and therefore cannot test the mapfile solution.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Conclusion
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             It looks like, for the most part, it's difficult to improve upon the
             <code>
              head
             </code>
             <code>
              tail
             </code>
             solution. At best the
             <code>
              sed
             </code>
             solution provides a ~3% increase in efficiency.
            </p>
            <p>
             (percentages calculated with the formula
             <code>
              % = (runtime/baseline - 1) * 100
             </code>
             )
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Row 50,000,000
             </strong>
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              00:01:12.705 (-00:00:02.616 = -3.47%)
              <code>
               sed
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              00:01:13.146 (-00:00:02.175 = -2.89%)
              <code>
               perl
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              00:01:15.321 (+00:00:00.000 = +0.00%)
              <code>
               head|tail
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              00:01:16.583 (+00:00:01.262 = +1.68%)
              <code>
               awk
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              00:05:12.156 (+00:03:56.835 = +314.43%)
              <code>
               cut
              </code>
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Row 500,000,000
             </strong>
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              00:12:07.050 (-00:00:26.160)
              <code>
               sed
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              00:12:11.460 (-00:00:21.750)
              <code>
               perl
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              00:12:33.210 (+00:00:00.000)
              <code>
               head|tail
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              00:12:45.830 (+00:00:12.620)
              <code>
               awk
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              00:52:01.560 (+00:40:31.650)
              <code>
               cut
              </code>
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Row 3,338,559,320
             </strong>
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              01:20:54.599 (-00:03:05.327)
              <code>
               sed
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              01:21:24.045 (-00:02:25.227)
              <code>
               perl
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              01:23:49.273 (+00:00:00.000)
              <code>
               head|tail
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              01:25:13.548 (+00:02:35.735)
              <code>
               awk
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              05:47:23.026 (+04:24:26.246)
              <code>
               cut
              </code>
             </li>
            </ol>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="21279361">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>

            </div>

             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/21279361/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             With
             <code>
              awk
             </code>
             it is pretty fast:
            </p>
            <pre><code>awk 'NR == num_line' file
</code></pre>
            <p>
             When this is true, the default behaviour of
             <code>
              awk
             </code>
             is performed:
             <code>
              {print $0}
             </code>
             .
            </p>
            <hr/>
            <h3>
             Alternative versions
            </h3>
            <p>
             If your file happens to be huge, you'd better
             <code>
              exit
             </code>
             after reading the required line. This way you save CPU time
             <sup>
              See time comparison at the end of the answer
             </sup>
             .
            </p>
            <pre><code>awk 'NR == num_line {print; exit}' file
</code></pre>
            <p>
             If you want to give the line number from a bash variable you can use:
            </p>
            <pre><code>awk 'NR == n' n=$num file
awk -v n=$num 'NR == n' file   # equivalent
</code></pre>
            <hr/>
            <p>
             See how much time is saved by using
             <code>
              exit
             </code>
             , specially if the line happens to be in the first part of the file:
            </p>
            <pre><code># Let's create a 10M lines file
for ((i=0; i&lt;100000; i++)); do echo "bla bla"; done &gt; 100Klines
for ((i=0; i&lt;100; i++)); do cat 100Klines; done &gt; 10Mlines

$ time awk 'NR == 1234567 {print}' 10Mlines
bla bla

real    0m1.303s
user    0m1.246s
sys 0m0.042s
$ time awk 'NR == 1234567 {print; exit}' 10Mlines
bla bla

real    0m0.198s
user    0m0.178s
sys 0m0.013s
</code></pre>
            <p>
             So the difference is 0.198s vs 1.303s, around 6x times faster.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

                 This method is always going to be slower because awk attempts to do field splitting. The overhead of field splitting can be reduced by
                 <code>
                  awk 'BEGIN{FS=RS}(NR == num_line) {print; exit}' file
                 </code>
                </span>

                <span class="comment-copy">
                 The real power of awk in this method comes forth when you want to concatenate line n1 of file1, n2 of file2, n3 or file3 ...
                 <code>
                  awk 'FNR==n' n=10 file1 n=30 file2 n=60 file3
                 </code>
                 . With GNU awk this can be sped up using
                 <code>
                  awk 'FNR==n{print;nextfile}' n=10 file1 n=30 file2 n=60 file3
                 </code>
                 .
                </span>

        <a name="45416880">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="45416880" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="6022384" data-position-on-page="5" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="40" id="answer-45416880" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="45416880">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="40" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             40
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/45416880/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             According to my tests, in terms of performance and readability my recommendation is:
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              tail -n+N | head -1
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              N
             </code>
             is the line number that you want. For example,
             <code>
              tail -n+7 input.txt | head -1
             </code>
             will print the 7th line of the file.
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              tail -n+N
             </code>
             will print everything starting from line
             <code>
              N
             </code>
             , and
             <code>
              head -1
             </code>
             will make it stop after one line.
            </p>
            <hr/>
            <p>
             The alternative
             <code>
              head -N | tail -1
             </code>
             is perhaps slightly more readable. For example, this will print the 7th line:
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              head -7 input.txt | tail -1
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             When it comes to performance, there is not much difference for smaller sizes, but it will be outperformed by the
             <code>
              tail | head
             </code>
             (from above) when the files become huge.
            </p>
            <p>
             The top-voted
             <code>
              sed 'NUMq;d'
             </code>
             is interesting to know, but I would argue that it will be understood by fewer people out of the box than the head/tail solution and it is also slower than tail/head.
            </p>
            <p>
             In my tests, both tails/heads versions outperformed
             <code>
              sed 'NUMq;d'
             </code>
             consistently. That is in line with the other benchmarks that were posted. It is hard to find a case where tails/heads was really bad. It is also not surprising, as these are operations that you would expect to be heavily optimized in a modern Unix system.
            </p>
            <p>
             To get an idea about the performance differences, these are the number that I get for a huge file (9.3G):
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              <code>
               tail -n+N | head -1
              </code>
              : 3.7 sec
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               head -N | tail -1
              </code>
              : 4.6 sec
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               sed Nq;d
              </code>
              : 18.8 sec
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             Results may differ, but the performance
             <code>
              head | tail
             </code>
             and
             <code>
              tail | head
             </code>
             is, in general, comparable for smaller inputs, and
             <code>
              sed
             </code>
             is always slower by a significant factor (around 5x or so).
            </p>
            <p>
             To reproduce my benchmark, you can try the following, but be warned that it will create a 9.3G file in the current working directory:
            </p>
            <pre><code>#!/bin/bash
readonly file=tmp-input.txt
readonly size=1000000000
readonly pos=500000000
readonly retries=3

seq 1 $size &gt; $file
echo "*** head -N | tail -1 ***"
for i in $(seq 1 $retries) ; do
    time head "-$pos" $file | tail -1
done
echo "-------------------------"
echo
echo "*** tail -n+N | head -1 ***"
echo

seq 1 $size &gt; $file
ls -alhg $file
for i in $(seq 1 $retries) ; do
    time tail -n+$pos $file | head -1
done
echo "-------------------------"
echo
echo "*** sed Nq;d ***"
echo

seq 1 $size &gt; $file
ls -alhg $file
for i in $(seq 1 $retries) ; do
    time sed $pos'q;d' $file
done
/bin/rm $file
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Here is the output of a run on my machine (ThinkPad X1 Carbon with an SSD and 16G of memory). I assume in the final run everything will come from the cache, not from disk:
            </p>
            <pre><code>*** head -N | tail -1 ***
500000000

real    0m9,800s
user    0m7,328s
sys     0m4,081s
500000000

real    0m4,231s
user    0m5,415s
sys     0m2,789s
500000000

real    0m4,636s
user    0m5,935s
sys     0m2,684s
-------------------------

*** tail -n+N | head -1 ***

-rw-r--r-- 1 phil 9,3G Jan 19 19:49 tmp-input.txt
500000000

real    0m6,452s
user    0m3,367s
sys     0m1,498s
500000000

real    0m3,890s
user    0m2,921s
sys     0m0,952s
500000000

real    0m3,763s
user    0m3,004s
sys     0m0,760s
-------------------------

*** sed Nq;d ***

-rw-r--r-- 1 phil 9,3G Jan 19 19:50 tmp-input.txt
500000000

real    0m23,675s
user    0m21,557s
sys     0m1,523s
500000000

real    0m20,328s
user    0m18,971s
sys     0m1,308s
500000000

real    0m19,835s
user    0m18,830s
sys     0m1,004s
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2017-07-31T13:10:02" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>
             <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
              <div class="js-post-menu pt2" data-post-id="45416880">

               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 Is performance different between
                 <code>
                  head | tail
                 </code>
                 vs
                 <code>
                  tail | head
                 </code>
                 ? Or does it depend on which line is being printed (beginning of file vs end of file)?
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/1081043/wisbucky" title="27,142 reputation">
                  wisbucky

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="83646457" data-comment-owner-id="783510" data-comment-score="1" id="comment-83646457">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="cool" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">
                 1
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 @wisbucky I have no hard figures, but one disadvantage of first using tail followed by a "head -1" is that you need to know the total length in advance. If you do not know it, you would have to count it first, which will be a loss performance-wise. Another disadvantage is that it is less intuitive to use. For instance, if you have the number 1 to 10 and you want to get the 3rd line, you would have to use "tail -8 | head -1". That is more error prone than "head -3 | tail -1".
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/783510/philipp-cla%c3%9fen" title="36,817 reputation">
                  Philipp Claßen
                 </a>

                <span class="comment-copy">
                 sorry, I should have included an example to be clear.
                 <code>
                  head -5 | tail -1
                 </code>
                 vs
                 <code>
                  tail -n+5 | head -1
                 </code>
                 . Actually, I found another answer that did a test comparison and found
                 <code>
                  tail | head
                 </code>
                 to be faster.
                 <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/48189289">
                  stackoverflow.com/a/48189289
                 </a>
                </span>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="6031029" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="6022384" data-position-on-page="6" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="28" id="answer-6031029" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="6031029">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="28" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             28
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/6031029/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

             </svg>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Wow, all the possibilities!
            </p>
            <p>
             Try this:
            </p>
            <pre><code>sed -n "${lineNum}p" $file
</code></pre>
            <p>
             or one of these depending upon your version of Awk:
            </p>
            <pre><code>awk  -vlineNum=$lineNum 'NR == lineNum {print $0}' $file
awk -v lineNum=4 '{if (NR == lineNum) {print $0}}' $file
awk '{if (NR == lineNum) {print $0}}' lineNum=$lineNum $file
</code></pre>
            <p>
             (
             <em>
              You may have to try the
              <code>
               nawk
              </code>
              or
              <code>
               gawk
              </code>
              command
             </em>
             ).
            </p>
            <p>
             Is there a tool that only does the print that particular line? Not one of the standard tools. However,
             <code>
              sed
             </code>
             is probably the closest and simplest to use.
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="23712058" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="6022384" data-position-on-page="7" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="21" id="answer-23712058" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="23712058">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="21" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             21
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/23712058/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             This question being tagged Bash, here's the Bash (≥4) way of doing: use
             <code>
              mapfile
             </code>
             with the
             <code>
              -s
             </code>
             (skip) and
             <code>
              -n
             </code>
             (count) option.
            </p>
            <p>
             If you need to get the 42nd line of a file
             <code>
              file
             </code>
             :
            </p>
            <pre><code>mapfile -s 41 -n 1 ary &lt; file
</code></pre>
            <p>
             At this point, you'll have an array
             <code>
              ary
             </code>
             the fields of which containing the lines of
             <code>
              file
             </code>
             (including the trailing newline), where we have skipped the first 41 lines (
             <code>
              -s 41
             </code>
             ), and stopped after reading one line (
             <code>
              -n 1
             </code>
             ). So that's really the 42nd line. To print it out:
            </p>
            <pre><code>printf '%s' "${ary[0]}"
</code></pre>
            <hr/>
            <p>
             If you need a range of lines, say the range 42–666 (inclusive), and say you don't want to do the math yourself, and print them on stdout:
            </p>
            <pre><code>mapfile -s $((42-1)) -n $((666-42+1)) ary &lt; file
printf '%s' "${ary[@]}"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             If you need to process these lines too, it's not really convenient to store the trailing newline. In this case use the
             <code>
              -t
             </code>
             option (trim):
            </p>
            <pre><code>mapfile -t -s $((42-1)) -n $((666-42+1)) ary &lt; file
# do stuff
printf '%s\n' "${ary[@]}"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             You can have a function do that for you:
            </p>
            <pre><code>print_file_range() {
    # $1-$2 is the range of file $3 to be printed to stdout
    local ary
    mapfile -s $(($1-1)) -n $(($2-$1+1)) ary &lt; "$3"
    printf '%s' "${ary[@]}"
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             No external commands, only Bash builtins!
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

             </time>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="67605064">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/67605064/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Save two keystrokes, print Nth line without using bracket:
            </p>
            <pre><code>sed  -n  Np  &lt;fileName&gt;
      ^   ^
       \   \___ 'p' for printing
        \______ '-n' for not printing by default 
</code></pre>
            <p>
             For example, to print 100th line:
            </p>
            <pre><code>sed -n 100p foo.txt      
</code></pre>
           </div>

             You may also used sed print and quit:
            </p>
            <pre><code>sed -n '10{p;q;}' file   # print line 10
</code></pre>

            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2011-05-17T11:49:24" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>
             <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
              <div class="js-post-menu pt2" data-post-id="6030326">
               <div class="d-flex gs8 s-anchors s-anchors__muted fw-wrap">

        <a name="48189289">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="48189289" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="6022384" data-position-on-page="11" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="7" id="answer-48189289" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="48189289">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="7" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             7
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/48189289/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             As a followup to CaffeineConnoisseur's very helpful benchmarking answer... I was curious as to how fast the 'mapfile' method was compared to others (as that wasn't tested), so I tried a quick-and-dirty speed comparison myself as I do have bash 4 handy. Threw in a test of the "tail | head" method (rather than head | tail) mentioned in one of the comments on the top answer while I was at it, as folks are singing its praises. I don't have anything nearly the size of the testfile used; the best I could find on short notice was a 14M pedigree file (long lines that are whitespace-separated, just under 12000 lines).
            </p>
            <p>
             Short version: mapfile appears faster than the cut method, but slower than everything else, so I'd call it a dud. tail | head, OTOH, looks like it could be the fastest, although with a file this size the difference is not all that substantial compared to sed.
            </p>
            <pre><code>$ time head -11000 [filename] | tail -1
[output redacted]

real    0m0.117s

$ time cut -f11000 -d$'\n' [filename]
[output redacted]

real    0m1.081s

$ time awk 'NR == 11000 {print; exit}' [filename]
[output redacted]

real    0m0.058s

$ time perl -wnl -e '$.== 11000 &amp;&amp; print &amp;&amp; exit;' [filename]
[output redacted]

real    0m0.085s

$ time sed "11000q;d" [filename]
[output redacted]

real    0m0.031s

$ time (mapfile -s 11000 -n 1 ary &lt; [filename]; echo ${ary[0]})
[output redacted]

real    0m0.309s

$ time tail -n+11000 [filename] | head -n1
[output redacted]

real    0m0.028s
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Hope this helps!
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2018-01-10T14:11:15" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>
             <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
              <div class="js-post-menu pt2" data-post-id="48189289">
               <div class="d-flex gs8 s-anchors s-anchors__muted fw-wrap">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="31468985" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="6022384" data-position-on-page="12" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="6" id="answer-31468985" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="31468985">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="6" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             6
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/31468985/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             The fastest solution for big files is always tail|head, provided that the two distances:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              from the start of the file to the starting line. Lets call it
              <code>
               S
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              the distance from the last line to the end of the file. Be it
              <code>
               E
              </code>
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             are known. Then, we could use this:
            </p>
            <pre><code>mycount="$E"; (( E &gt; S )) &amp;&amp; mycount="+$S"
howmany="$(( endline - startline + 1 ))"
tail -n "$mycount"| head -n "$howmany"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             howmany is just the count of lines required.
            </p>
            <p>
             Some more detail in
             <a href="https://unix.stackexchange.com/a/216614/79743">
              https://unix.stackexchange.com/a/216614/79743
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

        <a name="46707635">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="46707635" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="6022384" data-position-on-page="13" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="6" id="answer-46707635" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="46707635">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="6" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             6
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/46707635/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             All the above answers directly answer the question. But here's a less direct solution but a potentially more important idea, to provoke thought.
            </p>
            <p>
             Since line lengths are arbitrary, all the bytes of the file before the nth line
             <em>
              need
             </em>
             to be read. If you have a huge file or need to repeat this task many times, and this process is time-consuming, then you should seriously think about whether you should be storing your data in a different way in the first place.
            </p>
            <p>
             The real solution is to have an index, e.g. at the start of the file, indicating the positions where the lines begin. You could use a database format, or just add a table at the start of the file. Alternatively create a separate index file to accompany your large text file.
            </p>
            <p>
             e.g. you might create a list of character positions for newlines:
            </p>
            <pre><code>awk 'BEGIN{c=0;print(c)}{c+=length()+1;print(c+1)}' file.txt &gt; file.idx
</code></pre>
            <p>
             then read with
             <code>
              tail
             </code>
             , which actually
             <code>
              seek
             </code>
             s directly to the appropriate point in the file!
            </p>
            <p>
             e.g. to get line 1000:
            </p>
            <pre><code>tail -c +$(awk 'NR=1000' file.idx) file.txt | head -1
</code></pre>
            <ul>
             <li>
              This may not work with 2-byte / multibyte characters, since awk is "character-aware" but tail is not.
             </li>
             <li>
              I haven't tested this against a large file.
             </li>
             <li>
              Also see
              <a href="https://unix.stackexchange.com/a/8448/30032">
               this answer
              </a>
              .
             </li>
             <li>
              Alternatively - split your file into smaller files!
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2017-10-12T10:44:16" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="48303282" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="6022384" data-position-on-page="14" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="4" id="answer-48303282" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="48303282">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

              </path>
             </svg>

            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="4" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             4
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>

            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/48303282/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Using what others mentioned, I wanted this to be a quick &amp; dandy function in my bash shell.
            </p>
            <p>
             Create a file:
             <code>
              ~/.functions
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             Add to it the contents:
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              getline() {
  line=$1
  sed $line'q;d' $2
}
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             Then add this to your
             <code>
              ~/.bash_profile
             </code>
             :
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              source ~/.functions
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             Now when you open a new bash window, you can just call the function as so:
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              getline 441 myfile.txt
             </code>
            </p>
           </div>

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="113921930" data-comment-owner-id="874188" data-comment-score="0" id="comment-113921930">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 There is no need to assign
                 <code>
                  $1
                 </code>
                 to another variable before using it, and you are clobbering any other global
                 <code>
                  line
                 </code>
                 .  In Bash, use
                 <code>
                  local
                 </code>
                 for function variables; but here, as stated already, probably just do
                 <code>
                  sed "$1d;q" "$2"
                 </code>
                 . (Notice also the quoting of
                 <code>
                  "$2"
                 </code>
                 .)
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –

          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="34660257">

             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">

             </svg>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you got multiple lines by delimited by \n (normally new line). You can use 'cut' as well:
            </p>
            <pre><code>echo "$data" | cut -f2 -d$'\n'
</code></pre>
            <p>
             You will get the 2nd line from the file.
             <code>
              -f3
             </code>
             gives you the 3rd line.
            </p>
           </div>

                 Can be also used to display multiple lines:
                 <code>
                  cat FILE | cut -f2,5 -d$'\n'
                 </code>
                 will display lines 2 and 5 of the FILE. (But it will not preserve the order.)
                </span>

             </div>

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/47354309/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Lots of good answers already. I personally go with awk. For convenience, if you use bash, just add the below to your
             <code>
              ~/.bash_profile
             </code>
             . And, the next time you log in (or if you source your .bash_profile after this update), you will have a new nifty "nth" function available to pipe your files through.
            </p>
            <p>
             Execute this or put it in your ~/.bash_profile (if using bash) and reopen bash (or execute
             <code>
              source ~/.bach_profile
             </code>
             )
            </p>
            <pre class="lang-sh prettyprint-override"><code># print just the nth piped in line
nth () { awk -vlnum=${1} 'NR==lnum {print; exit}'; } 
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Then, to use it, simply pipe through it. E.g.,:
            </p>
            <pre><code>$ yes line | cat -n | nth 5
     5  line
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2017-11-17T15:42:57" itemprop="dateCreated">

             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             To print nth line using sed with a variable as line number:
            </p>
            <pre><code>a=4
sed -e $a'q:d' file
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Here the '-e' flag is for adding script to command to be executed.
            </p>
           </div>

        <a name="61747399">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="61747399" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="6022384" data-position-on-page="18" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="1" id="answer-61747399" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="61747399">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="1" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             1
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/61747399/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             After taking a look at
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/6022431/6320039">
              the top answer
             </a>
             and
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/48189289/6320039">
              the
             </a>
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/39217130/6320039">
              benchmark
             </a>
             , I've implemented a tiny helper function:
            </p>
            <pre class="lang-sh prettyprint-override"><code>function nth {
    if (( ${#} &lt; 1 || ${#} &gt; 2 )); then
        echo -e "usage: $0 \e[4mline\e[0m [\e[4mfile\e[0m]"
        return 1
    fi
    if (( ${#} &gt; 1 )); then
        sed "$1q;d" $2
    else
        sed "$1q;d"
    fi
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Basically you can use it in two fashions:
            </p>
            <pre class="lang-sh prettyprint-override"><code>nth 42 myfile.txt
do_stuff | nth 42
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2020-05-12T08:45:00" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="54405078" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="6022384" data-position-on-page="19" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="0" id="answer-54405078" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="54405078">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>
             </svg>

             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/54405078/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I've put some of the above answers into a short bash script that you can put into a file called
             <code>
              get.sh
             </code>
             and link to
             <code>
              /usr/local/bin/get
             </code>
             (or whatever other name you prefer).
            </p>
            <pre><code>#!/bin/bash
if [ "${1}" == "" ]; then
    echo "error: blank line number";
    exit 1
fi
re='^[0-9]+$'
if ! [[ $1 =~ $re ]] ; then
    echo "error: line number arg not a number";
    exit 1
fi
if [ "${2}" == "" ]; then
    echo "error: blank file name";
    exit 1
fi
sed "${1}q;d" $2;
exit 0
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Ensure it's executable with
            </p>
            <pre><code>$ chmod +x get
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Link it to make it available on the
             <code>
              PATH
             </code>
             with
            </p>
            <pre><code>$ ln -s get.sh /usr/local/bin/get
</code></pre>
           </div>
